    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div id="review_3067362367" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3067362367" />
    <a title="Stan Holcomb" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/106136044-stan-holcomb"><img alt="Stan Holcomb" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3067362367?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stan Holcomb" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stan Holcomb" href="/user/show/106136044-stan-holcomb">Stan Holcomb</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3067362367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1492200467914478567">Highly Recommended for: Book Clubs! We chose this book for our book club in the month of November 2019. What stood out the most to me was that although it was based on biblical facts, 95% was information that we never came across before (at least not knowingly). The facts and details represented were of pristine genuousness. They are brought about in a way that was understandable and through all of the different directions the author takes us in the many chapters, everything went together in per</span>
  <span id="freeText1492200467914478567" style="display:none">Highly Recommended for: Book Clubs! We chose this book for our book club in the month of November 2019. What stood out the most to me was that although it was based on biblical facts, 95% was information that we never came across before (at least not knowingly). The facts and details represented were of pristine genuousness. They are brought about in a way that was understandable and through all of the different directions the author takes us in the many chapters, everything went together in perfect harmony connecting to one another. I've went to church all of my life and most of these facts were never brought to my attention. This book was written with careful design and outstanding facts that are not known by most Christians. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1492200467914478567" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('g3F9M/KzandX5lJ4fjeasx7jwMz2fskGlbtAeiS3yyzUnFkd9QNmdeZWLo4EcVWE8OsM3/CG4sVmM8dvV/HGQw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KmxCJ5KOuOLBpDv+jzO10tn5kQ+VqbhW5mYq3HnlGrV9gWYJlT604HAURwj1dXrlN/FdHJNRk5UV7q3JCqMX2g==')})
  }
